    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6

# Radius of a shape #
type Radius = Float in

# Side length of a shape #
type SideLength = Float in

# Height of a shape #
type Height = Float in

# Common 3D shapes #
type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s

# Radius of a shape #
type Radius = Float in

# Side length of a shape #
type SideLength = Float in

# Height of a shape #
type Height = Float in

# Common 3D shapes #
type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #

    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s

# Side length of a shape #
type SideLength = Float in

# Height of a shape #
type Height = Float in

# Common 3D shapes #
type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s
        | Cyl

# Radius of a shape #
type Radius = Float in

# Side length of a shape #
type SideLength = Float in

# Height of a shape #
type Height = Float in

# Common 3D shapes #
type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s
        | Cylinder(r, h) => 2

# Radius of a shape #
type Radius = Float in

# Side length of a shape #
type SideLength = Float in

# Height of a shape #
type Height = Float in

# Common 3D shapes #
type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s
        | Cylinder(r, h) => 2.0 *

# Height of a shape #

# Common 3D shapes #

  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s
        | Cylinder(r, h) => 2.0 * pi *

    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s
        | Cylinder(r, h) => 2.0 * pi * r

# Radius of a shape #
type Radius = Float in

# Side length of a shape #
type SideLength = Float in

# Height of a shape #
type Height = Float in

# Common 3D shapes #
type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s
        | Cylinder(r, h) => 2.0 * pi * r * (r + h)

# Radius of a shape #
type Radius = Float in

# Side length of a shape #
type SideLength = Float in

# Height of a shape #
type Height = Float in

# Common 3D shapes #
type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

# Calculate the surface area of a shape #
let surface_area : Shape -> Float =
    fun s ->
        case s
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 * pi * r * r
        | Cube(s) => 6.0 * s * s
        | Cylinder(r, h) => 2.0 * pi * r * (r + h) end in
